Sir,

Certification audit on the annual accounts of National Institute of Technology (NIT),
Agartala for the year ended 31" March 2049 was taken up by this office under Section 19 (2)
of the Comptroller and Auditor General’s (Duties, Power & Conditions of Service} Act, 1971.
A Separate Audit Report (SAR) incorporating final cormments of the CRAG is issued along
with this letter. Apart from the audit comments Issued in SAR, audit has noticed 41 points
which required management’s actlon ta ensure compliance to the instructions of MHRD
with respect to preparation of annual accounts.
